        enum FieldState
        {
            NotStarted,         // There is no field under construction, either at the beginning of a line, or between fields.
            InProgress,         // A field is under construction. The last character or delimiter has yet to be found.
            Finished,           // The whole line is done.
        }   // enum FieldState

        {
            Unguarded,          // There are currently no unmatched quotes.
            GuardedField,       // The first character of the current field is a guard character.
            GuardedSegment,     // A guard character was found in the middle of a field.
        }   // enum GuardState
